\index{crosshairCursor@{crosshairCursor}!index.js@{index.js}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{crosshairCursor()}{crosshairCursor()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily function crosshair\+Cursor (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{options = {\ttfamily \{\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Returns an extension that turns the pointer cursor into a crosshair when a given modifier key, defaulting to Alt, is held down. 

Can serve as a visual hint that rectangular selection is going to happen when paired with \href{https://codemirror.net/6/docs/ref/\#view.rectangularSelection}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily rectangular\+Selection}}}. \mbox{\Hypertarget{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_aa84462c899004abae93a389608bfcfd0}\label{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_aa84462c899004abae93a389608bfcfd0}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_a468bdac05a86b6dc5a90cc6e3452e5be}\label{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_a468bdac05a86b6dc5a90cc6e3452e5be}} 
\index{index.js@{index.js}!drawSelection@{drawSelection}}
\index{drawSelection@{drawSelection}!index.js@{index.js}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{drawSelection()}{drawSelection()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily function draw\+Selection (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{config = {\ttfamily \{\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Returns an extension that hides the browser\textquotesingle{}s native selection and cursor, replacing the selection with a background behind the text (with the {\ttfamily cm-\/selection\+Background} class), and the cursors with elements overlaid over the code (using {\ttfamily cm-\/cursor-\/primary} and {\ttfamily cm-\/cursor-\/secondary}). 

This allows the editor to display secondary selection ranges, and tends to produce a type of selection more in line with that users expect in a text editor (the native selection styling will often leave gaps between lines and won\textquotesingle{}t fill the horizontal space after a line when the selection continues past it).

It does have a performance cost, in that it requires an extra D\+OM layout cycle for many updates (the selection is drawn based on D\+OM layout information that\textquotesingle{}s only available after laying out the content). \mbox{\Hypertarget{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_a37aa52d41236215a248f3b928b6c8174}\label{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_a37aa52d41236215a248f3b928b6c8174}} 
\index{index.js@{index.js}!dropCursor@{dropCursor}}
\index{dropCursor@{dropCursor}!index.js@{index.js}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{dropCursor()}{dropCursor()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily function drop\+Cursor (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Draws a cursor at the current drop position when something is dragged over the editor. 

\mbox{\Hypertarget{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_a30295b36fe01fb913ae7802305b7a754}\label{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_a30295b36fe01fb913ae7802305b7a754}}

Define an editor gutter. 

The order in which the gutters appear is determined by their extension priority. \mbox{\Hypertarget{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_afee5380e28ea0d527f96388341a8343e}\label{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_afee5380e28ea0d527f96388341a8343e}}

\index{gutters@{gutters}!index.js@{index.js}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{gutters()}{gutters()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily function gutters (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{config }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



The gutter-\/drawing plugin is automatically enabled when you add a gutter, but you can use this function to explicitly configure it. 

Unless {\ttfamily fixed} is explicitly set to {\ttfamily false}, the gutters are fixed, meaning they don\textquotesingle{}t scroll along with the content horizontally (except on Internet Explorer, which doesn\textquotesingle{}t support C\+SS \href{https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/CSS/position\#sticky}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily position\+: sticky}}}). \mbox{\Hypertarget{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_a46d3637d03c5b7e73b388e1185920758}\label{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_a46d3637d03c5b7e73b388e1185920758}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_afd3ad1f630e9f70c5714e6b634caa7a6}\label{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_afd3ad1f630e9f70c5714e6b634caa7a6}} 
\index{index.js@{index.js}!hoverTooltip@{hoverTooltip}}
\index{hoverTooltip@{hoverTooltip}!index.js@{index.js}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{hoverTooltip()}{hoverTooltip()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily function hover\+Tooltip (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{source,  }\item[{}]{options = {\ttfamily \{\}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set up a hover tooltip, which shows up when the pointer hovers over ranges of text. 

The callback is called when the mouse hovers over the document text. It should, if there is a tooltip associated with position {\ttfamily pos}, return the tooltip description (either directly or in a promise). The {\ttfamily side} argument indicates on which side of the position the pointer is—it will be -\/1 if the pointer is before the position, 1 if after the position.

Note that all hover tooltips are hosted within a single tooltip container element. This allows multiple tooltips over the same range to be \char`\"{}merged\char`\"{} together without overlapping. \mbox{\Hypertarget{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_ab016df8f99868364c18b696983318da8}\label{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_ab016df8f99868364c18b696983318da8}}

\index{index.js@{index.js}!logException@{logException}}
\index{logException@{logException}!index.js@{index.js}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{logException()}{logException()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily function log\+Exception (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{state,  }\item[{}]{exception,  }\item[{}]{context }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Log or report an unhandled exception in client code. 

Should probably only be used by extension code that allows client code to provide functions, and calls those functions in a context where an exception can\textquotesingle{}t be propagated to calling code in a reasonable way (for example when in an event handler).

Either calls a handler registered with \href{https://codemirror.net/6/docs/ref/\#view.EditorView^exceptionSink}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily Editor\+View.\+exception\+Sink}}}, {\ttfamily window.\+onerror}, if defined, or {\ttfamily console.\+error} (in which case it\textquotesingle{}ll pass {\ttfamily context}, when given, as first argument). \mbox{\Hypertarget{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_af550dc6cfd67b53afc24c0b692bfff7b}\label{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_af550dc6cfd67b53afc24c0b692bfff7b}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{rectangularSelection()}{rectangularSelection()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily function rectangular\+Selection (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{options }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Create an extension that enables rectangular selections. 

By default, it will react to left mouse drag with the Alt key held down. When such a selection occurs, the text within the rectangle that was dragged over will be selected, as one selection \href{https://codemirror.net/6/docs/ref/\#state.SelectionRange}{\texttt{ range}} per line. \mbox{\Hypertarget{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_ad2b042dce9ba514c31f09a5f155f0a99}\label{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_ad2b042dce9ba514c31f09a5f155f0a99}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{scrollPastEnd()}{scrollPastEnd()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily function scroll\+Past\+End (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Returns an extension that makes sure the content has a bottom margin equivalent to the height of the editor, minus one line height, so that every line in the document can be scrolled to the top of the editor. 

This is only meaningful when the editor is scrollable, and should not be enabled in editors that take the size of their content. \mbox{\Hypertarget{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_a7114fcfbb8c34f22c4d95e5a24703e6b}\label{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_a7114fcfbb8c34f22c4d95e5a24703e6b}}

\index{index.js@{index.js}!announce@{announce}}
\index{announce@{announce}!index.js@{index.js}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{announce}{announce}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classEditorView}{Editor\+View}} announce = \mbox{\hyperlink{classStateEffect_a3d82eba7534049621724ba9bad1091dd}{State\+Effect.\+define}}()}



\mbox{\hyperlink{classState}{State}} effect used to include screen reader announcements in a transaction. 

These will be added to the D\+OM in a visually hidden element with {\ttfamily aria-\/live=\char`\"{}polite\char`\"{}} set, and should be used to describe effects that are visually obvious but may not be noticed by screen reader users (such as moving to the next search match). \mbox{\Hypertarget{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_a3711546d7473b9a1a9f2dd3129b460ad}\label{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_a3711546d7473b9a1a9f2dd3129b460ad}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_a4cd1e5e47749d90d13587ddb06df4b46}\label{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_a4cd1e5e47749d90d13587ddb06df4b46}} 
\index{index.js@{index.js}!atomicRanges@{atomicRanges}}
\index{atomicRanges@{atomicRanges}!index.js@{index.js}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{atomicRanges}{atomicRanges}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classEditorView}{Editor\+View}} atomic\+Ranges = \mbox{\hyperlink{classFacet_a4fe323937f1a9d21c67b0d1c2f75ba9f}{Facet.\+define}}()}



Used to provide ranges that should be treated as atoms as far as cursor motion is concerned. 

This causes methods like \href{https://codemirror.net/6/docs/ref/\#view.EditorView.moveByChar}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily move\+By\+Char}}} and \href{https://codemirror.net/6/docs/ref/\#view.EditorView.moveVertically}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily move\+Vertically}}} (and the commands built on top of them) to skip across such regions when a selection endpoint would enter them. This does {\itshape not} prevent direct programmatic \href{https://codemirror.net/6/docs/ref/\#state.TransactionSpec.selection}{\texttt{ selection updates}} from moving into such regions. \mbox{\Hypertarget{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_a0043ca5b9efb6b09f1391d555826ee3f}\label{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_a0043ca5b9efb6b09f1391d555826ee3f}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily const current\+Platform = browser.\+mac ? \char`\"{}mac\char`\"{} \+: browser.\+windows ? \char`\"{}win\char`\"{} \+: browser.\+linux ? \char`\"{}linux\char`\"{} \+: \char`\"{}key\char`\"{}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_a78a00cca399b5a5911826ecc5f8f527b}\label{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_a78a00cca399b5a5911826ecc5f8f527b}} 
\index{index.js@{index.js}!darkTheme@{darkTheme}}
\index{darkTheme@{darkTheme}!index.js@{index.js}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{darkTheme}{darkTheme}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classEditorView}{Editor\+View}} dark\+Theme = \mbox{\hyperlink{classFacet_a4fe323937f1a9d21c67b0d1c2f75ba9f}{Facet.\+define}}(\{ combine\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{underscore_2underscore_8js_af19aa221cc4a953ad6addb0b03162a1c}{values}} =$>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{lodash_2indexOf_8js_a7e29ae897b51a9f825c50ee54704db7b}{values.\+index\+Of}}(true) $>$ -\/1 \})}



This facet records whether a dark theme is active. 

The extension returned by \href{https://codemirror.net/6/docs/ref/\#view.EditorView^theme}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily theme}}} automatically includes an instance of this when the {\ttfamily dark} option is set to true. \mbox{\Hypertarget{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_a724a2942332593e075e80db71e54c7ad}\label{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_a724a2942332593e075e80db71e54c7ad}} 
\index{index.js@{index.js}!decorations@{decorations}}
\index{decorations@{decorations}!index.js@{index.js}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{decorations}{decorations}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classEditorView}{Editor\+View}} decorations = \mbox{\hyperlink{classFacet_a4fe323937f1a9d21c67b0d1c2f75ba9f}{Facet.\+define}}()}



A facet that determines which \href{https://codemirror.net/6/docs/ref/\#view.Decoration}{\texttt{ decorations}} are shown in the view. 

Decorations can be provided in two ways—directly, or via a function that takes an editor view.

Only decoration sets provided directly are allowed to influence the editor\textquotesingle{}s vertical layout structure. The ones provided as functions are called {\itshape after} the new viewport has been computed, and thus {\bfseries{must not}} introduce block widgets or replacing decorations that cover line breaks.

If you want decorated ranges to behave like atomic units for cursor motion and deletion purposes, also provide the range set containing the decorations to \href{https://codemirror.net/6/docs/ref/\#view.EditorView^atomicRanges}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily Editor\+View.\+atomic\+Ranges}}}. \mbox{\Hypertarget{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_a0dfa8300c8daf8e4b6b82ad7450ae960}\label{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_a0dfa8300c8daf8e4b6b82ad7450ae960}} 
\index{index.js@{index.js}!DefaultPlaceholder@{DefaultPlaceholder}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{classFacet}{Facet}} that controls whether the editor content D\+OM is editable. 

When its highest-\/precedence value is {\ttfamily false}, the element will not have its {\ttfamily contenteditable} attribute set. (Note that this doesn\textquotesingle{}t affect A\+PI calls that change the editor content, even when those are bound to keys or buttons. Allows you to provide a function that should be called when the library catches an exception from an extension (mostly from view plugins, but may be used by other extensions to route exceptions from user-\/code-\/provided callbacks).

\mbox{\hyperlink{classFacet}{Facet}} used to add a class to all gutter elements for a given line. 

Markers given to this facet should {\itshape only} define an \href{https://codemirror.net/6/docs/ref/\#view.GutterMarker.elementClass}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily elementclass}}}, not a \href{https://codemirror.net/6/docs/ref/\#view.GutterMarker.toDOM}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily to\+D\+OM}}} (or the marker will appear in all gutters for the line). \mbox{\Hypertarget{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_a66d662449e51b931b2da8a4462f653ec}\label{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_a66d662449e51b931b2da8a4462f653ec}}

\index{index.js@{index.js}!inputHandler@{inputHandler}}
\index{inputHandler@{inputHandler}!index.js@{index.js}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{inputHandler}{inputHandler}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classEditorView}{Editor\+View}} input\+Handler = \mbox{\hyperlink{classFacet_a4fe323937f1a9d21c67b0d1c2f75ba9f}{Facet.\+define}}()}



An input handler can override the way changes to the editable D\+OM content are handled. 

Handlers are passed the document positions between which the change was found, and the new content. When one returns true, no further input handlers are called and the default behavior is prevented. \mbox{\Hypertarget{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_a359ea6784f4eb1480fd49a2a9c30249b}\label{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_a359ea6784f4eb1480fd49a2a9c30249b}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{classFacet}{Facet}} used for registering keymaps. 

You can add multiple keymaps to an editor. Their priorities determine their precedence (the ones specified early or with high priority get checked first). \doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{lineWrapping}{lineWrapping}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{perLineTextDirection}{perLineTextDirection}}

{\bfseries Initial value\+:}
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}

\DoxyCodeLine{\})}

\end{DoxyCode}


By default, the editor assumes all its content has the same \href{https://codemirror.net/6/docs/ref/\#view.Direction}{\texttt{ text direction}}. 

Configure this with a {\ttfamily true} value to make it read the text direction of every (rendered) line separately. \mbox{\Hypertarget{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_a43b7a606f4b3f0c86f2f3ed5066658dc}\label{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_a43b7a606f4b3f0c86f2f3ed5066658dc}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{classFacet}{Facet}} that allows extensions to provide additional scroll margins (space around the sides of the scrolling element that should be considered invisible). 

This can be useful when the plugin introduces elements that cover part of that element (for example a horizontally fixed gutter). \mbox{\Hypertarget{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_a8a2237ad87cc253940874488109e593b}\label{_0dcodemirror_2view_2dist_2index_8js_a8a2237ad87cc253940874488109e593b}}
